{"answers": ["An elevator with a counterbalance"], "model_answer": "A real-world application of an Atwood machine is an elevator with a counterbalance. An elevator with a counterbalance approximates an ideal Atwood machine and thereby relieves the driving motor from the load of holding the elevator cab - it has to overcome only the weight difference and inertia of the two masses. This design allows the elevator to move smoothly and efficiently, reducing the load on the motor and increasing the overall performance of the system."}
